This patch improves the performance of the DefaultKeyedValues by replacing the single combined key-value-list with separate lists for keys and values and by adding a key-to-index mapping for faster lookups.   The implementation behaves a lot faster for read operations and for plain add operations. It greatly sucks for insert-operations and sort operations. But people who sort the data after each insert should be shot anyway or  should implement a better suited version.  
Argh, seems we are using org.jfree.chart.util.SortOrder now instead of the JCommon version.   
Old jar needs to be removed. 
The old iText 2.0.6 jar was just the HTML document for the download page. This one is better. 
Don't import from JCommon.
Renamed 'keyToValueMapping' --> 'indexMap' and fixed Eclipse warnings.
